#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Merge File1 (base student data) with File2 (supplemental student numbers).
Generates File5 with complete student records and temp IDs for missing XH.
"""
import csv
import json
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Dict, List, Set
import sys

# Add scripts dir to path
sys.path.insert(0, str(Path(__file__).parent))
from generate_temp_user_ids import determine_user_id
from normalize_colleges import normalize_college_name


def load_file2_by_key(file2_path: str) -> Dict[str, dict]:
    """Load File2 and index by (name + normalized_college + BH) key."""
    file2_index = {}

    with open(file2_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        reader = csv.DictReader(f)
        for row in reader:
            name = row['XM'].strip()
            college_raw = row['FY'].strip()
            bh = row['BH'].strip()

            try:
                college_norm = normalize_college_name(college_raw)
            except ValueError:
                continue  # Skip if college can't be normalized

            key = f"{name}|{college_norm}|{bh}"
            file2_index[key] = row

    return file2_index


def merge_files(file1_path: str, file2_path: str, output_path: str) -> dict:
    """
    Merge File1 and File2, generate File5 with complete student data.

    Returns merge report with statistics.
    """
    file2_index = load_file2_by_key(file2_path)

    stats = {
        'total_file1_rows': 0,
        'matched_count': 0,
        'file1_only_count': 0,
        'file2_only_count': 0,
        'grad_generated_ids': 0,
        'tmp_generated_ids': 0,
        'normalization_failures': 0,
        'skipped_rows': []
    }

    output_rows = []
    matched_file2_keys = set()  # Track matched File2 rows

    with open(file1_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        reader = csv.DictReader(f)

        for row_idx, row in enumerate(reader, start=1):
            stats['total_file1_rows'] += 1

            # Extract File1 fields
            name = row['学生姓名'].strip()
            college_raw = row['学院名称'].strip()
            building = row['楼栋名称'].strip()
            room = row['寝室号'].strip()
            major = row['专业'].strip()
            grade = row['年级'].strip()
            class_name = row['班级'].strip()
            level = row['层次'].strip()  # 本科/硕士/博士

            # Normalize college
            try:
                college_norm = normalize_college_name(college_raw)
            except ValueError:
                stats['normalization_failures'] += 1
                stats['skipped_rows'].append({
                    'row': row_idx,
                    'name': name,
                    'college': college_raw,
                    'reason': 'college_normalization_failed'
                })
                continue

            # Try to match with File2
            match_key = f"{name}|{college_norm}|{class_name}"
            file2_row = file2_index.get(match_key)

            # Track matched File2 keys
            if file2_row:
                matched_file2_keys.add(match_key)

            # Determine if graduate student
            is_graduate = level in ['硕士', '博士']

            # Get student_no and generate user_id
            student_no = file2_row['XH'].strip() if file2_row else None
            user_id, user_id_source = determine_user_id(
                student_no=student_no,
                name=name,
                college=college_norm,
                building=building,
                room=room,
                row_index=row_idx,
                is_graduate=is_graduate
            )

            # Update statistics
            if file2_row:
                stats['matched_count'] += 1
            else:
                stats['file1_only_count'] += 1
                if user_id_source == 'grad_generated':
                    stats['grad_generated_ids'] += 1
                elif user_id_source == 'tmp_generated':
                    stats['tmp_generated_ids'] += 1

            # Build output row
            output_row = {
                'source_row_id': row_idx,
                'user_id': user_id,
                'user_id_source': user_id_source,
                'student_no': student_no or '',
                'name': name,
                'department': college_norm,
                'major': major,
                'grade': grade,
                'class_id': class_name,
                'level': level,
                'building_name': building,
                'room_number': room,
                'phone': file2_row.get('SJHM', '').strip() if file2_row else '',
                'email': file2_row.get('email', '').strip() if file2_row else '',
            }

            output_rows.append(output_row)

    # Process File2-only rows (user decision: import them)
    for match_key, file2_row in file2_index.items():
        if match_key not in matched_file2_keys:
            stats['file2_only_count'] += 1

            # Parse match_key to get name, college, class
            name, college_norm, class_name = match_key.split('|')

            # Extract File2 data
            student_no = file2_row['XH'].strip()

            # File2-only row output
            output_row = {
                'source_row_id': f'FILE2_{stats["file2_only_count"]}',
                'user_id': student_no,
                'user_id_source': 'file2_only',
                'student_no': student_no,
                'name': name,
                'department': college_norm,
                'major': '',  # Not in File2
                'grade': '',  # Not in File2
                'class_id': class_name,
                'level': '',  # Not in File2
                'building_name': '',  # Not in File2
                'room_number': '',  # Not in File2
                'phone': file2_row.get('SJHM', '').strip(),
                'email': file2_row.get('email', '').strip(),
            }

            output_rows.append(output_row)

    # Write File5
    if output_rows:
        fieldnames = list(output_rows[0].keys())
        with open(output_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8', newline='') as f:
            writer = csv.DictWriter(f, fieldnames=fieldnames)
            writer.writeheader()
            writer.writerows(output_rows)

    return stats


if __name__ == "__main__":
    import argparse

    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description='Merge File1 and File2 to generate File5')
    parser.add_argument('--file1', required=True, help='Path to File1 CSV')
    parser.add_argument('--file2', required=True, help='Path to File2 CSV')
    parser.add_argument('--output', required=True, help='Output path for File5')
    parser.add_argument('--report', help='Optional merge report JSON output path')

    args = parser.parse_args()

    print(f"Merging {args.file1} + {args.file2} → {args.output}")

    stats = merge_files(args.file1, args.file2, args.output)

    print("\n=== Merge Report ===")
    print(f"Total File1 rows: {stats['total_file1_rows']}")
    print(f"Matched with File2: {stats['matched_count']}")
    print(f"File1 only: {stats['file1_only_count']}")
    print(f"  - Graduate IDs generated: {stats['grad_generated_ids']}")
    print(f"  - Temp IDs generated: {stats['tmp_generated_ids']}")
    print(f"File2 only: {stats['file2_only_count']}")
    print(f"Normalization failures: {stats['normalization_failures']}")
    print(f"Output rows: {stats['total_file1_rows'] + stats['file2_only_count'] - stats['normalization_failures']}")

    if stats['skipped_rows']:
        print(f"\n⚠️  Skipped {len(stats['skipped_rows'])} rows (see report)")

    if args.report:
        with open(args.report, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            json.dump(stats, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
        print(f"\nFull report saved to: {args.report}")

    print("\n✓ Merge completed")

   133	    if not serializer.is_valid():
   134	        return Response({'error': {'code': 'VALIDATION_ERROR', 'message': '请求参数验证失败',
   135	                                    'details': serializer.errors}},
   136	                        status=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST)
   137	
   138	    provider = MockDormCheckoutProvider()
   139	    dorm_status = provider.check_status(user.user_id)
   140	
   141	    if dorm_status.status != DormCheckoutStatus.COMPLETED:
   142	        return Response({'error': {'code': 'DORM_BLOCKED', 'message': '宿舍清退未完成，无法提交申请',
   143	                                    'details': {'student_id': user.user_id, 'dorm_status': dorm_status.status,
   144	                                                'blocking_reason': dorm_status.blocking_reason}}},
   145	                        status=status.HTTP_422_UNPROCESSABLE_ENTITY)
   146	
   147	    # Find all dorm managers for the building
   148	    dorm_managers = []
   149	    building = user.building
   150	
   151	    # Try to find dorm managers by building
   152	    if building and building.strip():
   153	        dorm_managers = list(User.objects.filter(
   154	            role=UserRole.DORM_MANAGER,
   155	            building=building,
   156	            active=True
   157	        ).order_by('user_id'))
   158	
   159	        if len(dorm_managers) > 1:
   160	            logging.info(
   161	                f"Multiple dorm managers found for building {building}: "
   162	                f"{len(dorm_managers)} managers. Creating approval for each."
   163	            )
   164	
   165	    # Fallback: use default dorm manager for students without building
   166	    if not dorm_managers:
   167	        from django.conf import settings
   168	        fallback_id = getattr(settings, 'FALLBACK_DORM_MANAGER_USER_ID', '92008149')
   169	        try:
   170	            fallback_manager = User.objects.get(role=UserRole.DORM_MANAGER, user_id=fallback_id, active=True)
   171	            dorm_managers = [fallback_manager]
   172	        except User.DoesNotExist:
   173	            return Response({'error': {'code': 'NOT_FOUND', 'message': '无可用宿管员',
   174	                                        'details': {'building': building or '未分配', 'fallback_id': fallback_id}}},
   175	                            status=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND)
   176	
   177	    application = Application.objects.create(
   178	        application_id=f'app_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}',
   179	        student=user,
   180	        student_name=user.name,
   181	        class_id=user.class_id,
   182	        reason=serializer.validated_data['reason'],
   183	        leave_date=serializer.validated_data['leave_date'],
   184	        status=ApplicationStatus.PENDING_DORM_MANAGER,
   185	        dorm_checkout_status=dorm_status.status
   186	    )
   187	
   188	    # Create approval for each dorm manager
   189	    for dorm_manager in dorm_managers:
   190	        dorm_manager_approval = Approval.objects.create(
   191	            approval_id=f'apv_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}',
   192	            application=application,
   193	            step=ApprovalStep.DORM_MANAGER,
   194	            approver=dorm_manager,
   195	            approver_name=dorm_manager.name,
   196	            decision=ApprovalDecision.PENDING
   197	        )
   198	        notify_application_submitted(application, dorm_manager_approval)
   199	
   200	    return Response(ApplicationSerializer(application).data, status=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)

    73	def validate_routing(file5_path: str, file3_path: str, file4_path: str) -> dict:
    74	    """
    75	    Validate that all students can be routed to approvers.
    76	
    77	    Returns validation report with coverage statistics.
    78	    """
    79	    students = load_students(file5_path)
    80	    building_managers = load_dorm_managers(file3_path)
    81	    dept_counselors = load_counselors(file4_path)
    82	
    83	    report = {
    84	        'total_students': len(students),
    85	        'dorm_manager_coverage': 0,
    86	        'counselor_coverage': 0,
    87	        'fully_routable': 0,
    88	        'missing_dorm_manager': [],
    89	        'missing_counselor': [],
    90	        'unroutable_students': []
    91	    }
    92	
    93	    for student in students:
    94	        user_id = student['user_id']
    95	        name = student['name']
    96	        building = student['building_name']
    97	        department = student['department']
    98	
    99	        # Check dorm manager routing
   100	        has_dorm_manager = building in building_managers
   101	        if has_dorm_manager:
   102	            report['dorm_manager_coverage'] += 1
   103	        else:
   104	            report['missing_dorm_manager'].append({
   105	                'user_id': user_id,
   106	                'name': name,
   107	                'building': building
   108	            })
   109	
   110	        # Check counselor routing
   111	        has_counselor = department in dept_counselors
   112	        if has_counselor:
   113	            report['counselor_coverage'] += 1
   114	        else:
   115	            report['missing_counselor'].append({
   116	                'user_id': user_id,
   117	                'name': name,
   118	                'department': department
   119	            })
   120	
   121	        # Check full routing
   122	        if has_dorm_manager and has_counselor:
   123	            report['fully_routable'] += 1
   124	        else:
   125	            report['unroutable_students'].append({
   126	                'user_id': user_id,
   127	                'name': name,
   128	                'building': building,
   129	                'department': department,
   130	                'missing': {
   131	                    'dorm_manager': not has_dorm_manager,
   132	                    'counselor': not has_counselor
   133	                }
   134	            })
   135	
   136	    # Calculate percentages
   137	    total = report['total_students']
   138	    report['dorm_manager_coverage_pct'] = (report['dorm_manager_coverage'] / total * 100) if total > 0 else 0
   139	    report['counselor_coverage_pct'] = (report['counselor_coverage'] / total * 100) if total > 0 else 0
   140	    report['fully_routable_pct'] = (report['fully_routable'] / total * 100) if total > 0 else 0
   141	
   142	    return report
   143

codex
**审查结论**

不建议把 `docs/硕士研究生-毕业生290人.xls` 仅按“学号/姓名”直接导入为可申请学生。当前系统运行路由依赖两段：

- 提交申请时按学生 `building` 找宿管员，找不到会走默认宿管员兜底：[backend/apps/applications/views.py](/home/caohui/projects/graduation-leave-system/backend/apps/applications/views.py:147)
- 宿管审批通过后按学生 `department` 找辅导员，找不到会返回 `404 该学院辅导员不存在`：[backend/apps/approvals/views.py](/home/caohui/projects/graduation-leave-system/backend/apps/approvals/views.py:213)
- `building`、`department` 在模型上可为空，但业务路由不完整：[backend/apps/users/models.py](/home/caohui/projects/graduation-leave-system/backend/apps/users/models.py:38)

**3个方案评估**

方案A：补充研究生楼栋/学院数据后导入  
最佳方案。优点是审批责任、数据审计、统计口径都正确，能通过现有路由覆盖校验逻辑。缺点是依赖数据源确认，短期推进慢。建议优先从 `1-5830名毕业生（含研究生）`、入住信息、学工系统/研究生管理系统按学号或姓名关联补齐。

方案B：研究生统一路由到特定辅导员  
可作为临时兜底，但必须有业务授权。技术上可以给研究生统一 `department=研究生院`，并配置一个对应辅导员；住宿侧若无楼栋，则依赖默认宿管员或统一研究生宿管员。风险是审批人可能不是实际责任人，日志合规性较弱，后续争议难解释。

方案C：研究生不纳入系统  
仅在业务明确“研究生不走该离校系统”时成立。否则这是已知遗漏，290人约4.6%，会导致系统覆盖率和毕业生总数口径不一致，也会让数据库报告继续显示错误结论。

**技术阻塞点**

最大阻塞不是导入本身，而是“导入后能不能走完整审批”。`department` 缺失会在宿管通过后卡住辅导员审批创建；`building` 缺失虽然有默认宿管兜底，但这和 `validate_routing_coverage.py` 的100%覆盖校验口径不一致：[backend/scripts/validate_routing_coverage.py](/home/caohui/projects/graduation-leave-system/backend/scripts/validate_routing_coverage.py:99)

另外，3列文件缺少 `is_graduating`、`graduation_year`、`class_id`。前两者可默认为 `true`、`2026`；`class_id` 当前运行路由不再主要依赖它，但申请快照会保存 `class_id`，建议设为 `GRAD-2026` 或尽量从外部系统补齐。

**推荐实施路径**

走“A为主，B为受控兜底”的两阶段方案：

1. 先把290人作为研究生候选清单，不直接全量激活导入。
2. 用学号优先、姓名+学院/住宿信息次之，关联现有 File1、入住数据、XG/研究生系统，补齐 `building`、`department`。
3. 对仍缺 `department` 的少量人员，不导入为可申请状态，或经业务确认统一映射到“研究生院”辅导员。
4. 对仍缺 `building` 的人员，优先补住宿楼栋；若业务确认可集中处理，再使用默认宿管员兜底，并在报告中标记。
5. 导入前扩展/复用路由覆盖校验，要求输出研究生覆盖率、兜底人数、不可路由人数。
6. 最后执行 dry-run、抽样提交申请、宿管通过、辅导员审批创建验证。

**工作量评估**

如果补充数据源已经可用：约 `6-10小时`。包括转换/清洗1-2h，关联补齐2-3h，导入脚本调整1-2h，路由校验和抽样测试2-3h。

如果需要等外部系统或人工确认楼栋/学院：技术工作仍是 `6-10小时`，但整体排期通常是 `1-3个工作日`，主要取决于数据确认。

如果采用方案B临时统一路由：约 `3-5小时`，但需要业务书面确认统一辅导员和宿管兜底规则。该方案适合临时验收，不适合作为最终数据方案。
